Cara membuat brownies= Oreo Tepyng Gula Aduk rata terus campur telur 3,terus dikasi air hangat 350-400 ml aduk rata hingga mengental,dikasi voklat yg habis di tim trus dikasi margarin yang di tim jga,campurkan dan aduk,tarus tambahkan baking soda setengah sendok teh,aduk kembali,terus di taroh didalam cetakan brownies nya,lalu oven hingga 30m-1jam hingga matang sambil dilihat lihat,taraa brwonies uda matang dan siap dimakan..:)

Did anyone else notice that the sculptures the boys are standing next to when they're performing "Life Goes On" literally symbolises their career/life in music.  *Jungkook - No More Dream 2014* (the school bus that Jin crashed the cardboard boxes with at the basketball court), *Jimin - Run 2015* (the two trains that they sat on and walked passed), *RM - Blood, Sweat and Tears 2016* (the second room in the beginning of the MV where Suga (love to have lil' meow meow back) places his hand over Jimins eyes) *Taehyung - DNA  2017* (the yellow metal structure that they danced in),  *Jin - Fake Love 2018* (i think that's where they filmed the Fake Love Official Teaser 1, correct me if I'm wrong),  *Suga - Boy With Luv 2019* (literally the beginning of the MV) and *J-hope - ON 2020* (the dance break in the MV where they began a cult lol) 💜💜💜
